SEE <s>kim</s> and 2. <s>kad</s> , and <cf/> the following words in which the interrogative base <s>ka</s> appears , <s>katama</s>,<s>katara</s>,<s>kati</s>,<s>kaTam</s>,<s>kadA</s>,<s>karhi</s>,<s>kA</s> , <etc/> , who? which? what? In its declension <s>ka</s> follows the pronoun <s>tad</s> except in nom. acc. sing. neut. , where <s>kim</s> has taken the place of <s>kad</s> or <s>kat</s> in classical <as0 type="ns">Sanskr2it</as0><as1>Sanskrit</as1>
41336.1,ka,H1A : X-3/30 : but the old form <s>kad</s> is found in the <as0>Veda</as0><as1><s>veda</s></as1> SEE  ; <b>cf. Zd. <etym>ka</etym> , <etym>ko7</etym> , <etym>kA7</etym> , <etym>kat</etym> ; Gk. <gk>1</gk> , <gk>2</gk> , Ion. <gk>3</gk> , <gk>4</gk> , <gk>5</gk> , <gk>6</gk> ; Lat. <etym>quis</etym> , <etym>quid</etym> ; Lith. <etym>kas</etym> <s>k/a</s> ; Goth. <etym>hvas</etym> , <etym>hvo7</etym> , <etym>hva</etym> , Angl.Sax. <etym>hwa1</etym> , <etym>hwaet</etym> ; Eng. <etym>who</etym> , <etym>what</etym>.</b> The interrogative sentence introduced by <s>ka</s> is often terminated by <s>iti</s> e.g. <s>kasya sa putra iti kaTyatAm</s> , let it be said , <quote> whose son is he? </quote> , but <s>iti</s> may be omitted and the sentence lose its direct interrogative character e.g. <s>kasya sa putro na jYAyate</s> , it is not known whose son he is . <s>ka</s> with or without 1. <s>as</s> may express <quote> how is it possible that? </quote> <quote> what power have I , you , they , <etc1/>? </quote> e.g. <s>ke mama Danvino'nye</s> , what can the other archers do against me? <s>ke AvAm paritrAtum</s> , what power have we to rescue you? <s>ka</s> is often connected with a demonstrative pron. e.g. <s>ko 'yam AyAti</s> , who comes here? or with the potential e.g. <s>ko hariM nindet</s> , who will blame <as0>Hari</as0><as1><s>hari</s></as1>? <s>ka</s> is sometimes repeated e.g. <s>kaH ko 'tra</s> , who is there? <s>kAn kAn</s> , whom? whom? i.e. which of them? cf. Gram. 54 , and the repetition is often due to a kind of attraction e.g. <s>kezAM kiM SAstram aDyayanIyam</s> , which book is to be read by whom? Gram. 836. <s>a</s>. When <s>kim</s> is connected with the inst. c. of a noun or with the indecl. participle it may express <quote> what is gained by doing so , <etc1/>? </quote> <eq/> <s>ko'rTas</s> Page240,3
41336.3,ka,H1A : X-5/30 : <s>vA</s> and <s>api</s> are not so common , but the latter is often found in classical <as0 type="ns">Sanskr2it</as0><as1>Sanskrit</as1> e.g. <s>kaScid</s> , any one ; <s>kecid</s> , some ; <s>na kaScid</s> , no one ; <s>na kiMcid api</s> , nothing whatsoever ; <s>yaH kaScid</s> , any one whatsoever ; <s>kecit</s> - <s>kecit</s> , some - others ; <s>yasmin kasmin vA deSe</s> , in any country whatsoever ; <s>na ko 'pi</s> , no one ; <s>na kimapi</s> , nothing whatever . <s>ka</s> may sometimes be used , like 2. <s>kad</s> , at the beginning of a compound.
